G2. keros_core.c — FIQ handler + governance lifecycle
------------------------------------------------------------------------

```c
/* keros_core.c
 * CORTEX PROTOCOL — Layer 1: FIQ Handler & Hardware Lifecycle (KEROS)
 * Target: ARMv8.5-A / TrustZone EL1-S bare-metal
 * Status: SPECIFICATION — Milestone 2 hardware target
 *
 * Handles governance snapshot lifecycle via hardware RTC interrupt.
 * On expiration or validation failure: purge registers, force Hi-Z,
 * enter low-power hold via WFI. Recovery only via biometric ResProtocol.
 */

#include "keros_types.h"

/* ── MMIO register map (platform-specific — Snapdragon 8 Gen 1) ──────────── *
 * These addresses are placeholders. Real values from BSP / device tree.
 * Replace with verified addresses from Qualcomm TRM before production. */
#define MMIO_RTC_TIMESTAMP     ((volatile uint64_t *) 0x3F004000ULL)
#define MMIO_HARDWARE_MUX_CTRL ((volatile uint32_t *) 0x3F005000ULL)
#define REG_MUX_HI_Z_FORCE     (1u << 31)

/* ── System state ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
#define STATE_INIT         0x00000000u
#define STATE_SOMA_SAFE    0x00000001u
#define STATE_SHIELD       0x00000002u
#define STATE_LOCK         0x00000003u
#define STATE_DUMMY        0x0000007Fu   /* Containment / isolation mode */

extern ExecutableSnapshot current_snapshot;   /* Provided by governance loader */
static volatile uint32_t  system_state = STATE_INIT;

/* ── Register purge — Spectre/Meltdown mitigation ───────────────────────── *
 * Clears caller-saved ABI registers (x0–x15) and NZCV flags.
 * Must be called before entering Hi-Z or WFI to prevent cache residue. */
static inline void __attribute__((always_inline)) purge_volatile_registers(void)
{
    __asm__ volatile (
        "mov x0,  #0 \n\t"
        "mov x1,  #0 \n\t"
        "mov x2,  #0 \n\t"
        "mov x3,  #0 \n\t"
        "mov x4,  #0 \n\t"
        "mov x5,  #0 \n\t"
        "mov x6,  #0 \n\t"
        "mov x7,  #0 \n\t"
        "mov x8,  #0 \n\t"
        "mov x9,  #0 \n\t"
        "mov x10, #0 \n\t"
        "mov x11, #0 \n\t"
        "mov x12, #0 \n\t"
        "mov x13, #0 \n\t"
        "mov x14, #0 \n\t"
        "mov x15, #0 \n\t"
        "msr nzcv, x0  \n\t"   /* Clear condition flags */
        "dsb sy        \n\t"   /* Full system memory barrier */
        "isb           \n\t"   /* Instruction barrier — flush pipeline */
        "csdb          \n\t"   /* Consumption Data Barrier — anti-Spectre v4 */
        :
        :
        : "x0","x1","x2","x3","x4","x5","x6","x7",
          "x8","x9","x10","x11","x12","x13","x14","x15",
          "memory"
    );
}

/* ── Governance snapshot expiry / failure handler ────────────────────────── *
 * Mapped as FIQ in TZASC — fires directly at EL3 Secure Monitor.
 * Execution: EL1-S (Secure World only). Normal World suspended.
 *
 * POST-CONDITION: CPU enters WFI loop. Only hardware pulse channel
 * remains active. Biometric ResProtocol required for recovery. */
void __attribute__((interrupt("FIQ"))) handle_secure_rtc_fiq(void)
{
    /* 1. Atomic RTC read — single 64-bit load, no branch on value */
    uint64_t now = *MMIO_RTC_TIMESTAMP;

    /* 2. Constant-time comparison using subtraction carry bit.
     *    No if/else — bitmask determines whether to purge.
     *    expired = 1 when now >= expiration_timestamp */
    uint64_t expiry  = current_snapshot.metadata.timestamp_expiration;
    uint64_t delta   = now - expiry;                   /* wraps if now < expiry */
    uint32_t expired = (uint32_t)(delta >> 63 ^ 1u);  /* 1 = expired, 0 = valid */

    /* 3. Unconditional path: state update via bitmask (no branch) */
    uint32_t new_state = STATE_SOMA_SAFE
                       | (expired * (STATE_DUMMY - STATE_SOMA_SAFE));
    system_state = new_state;

    /* 4. If not expired: return early (normal FIQ return) */
    if (!expired) {
        __asm__ volatile ("dsb sy\nisb" ::: "memory");
        return;
    }

    /* ── ISOLATION SEQUENCE (Article 19) ── */

    /* 5. Purge CPU registers — prevent forensic register extraction */
    purge_volatile_registers();

    /* 6. Force hardware bus to High-Z — physically disconnect sensor lines */
    *MMIO_HARDWARE_MUX_CTRL = REG_MUX_HI_Z_FORCE;
    __asm__ volatile ("dsb sy" ::: "memory");

    /* 7. Enter hardware low-power hold — WFI loop.
     *    CPU halts here. Only hardware RTC + pulse sensor remain active.
     *    Recovery: biometric ResProtocol (120s HF HRV window). */
    while (1) {
        __asm__ volatile ("wfi" ::: "memory");
    }
    /* Unreachable — no return from isolation */
}

```


------------------------------------------------------------------------
G3. biometric_filter.c — Phi operator: Db2 wavelet + Box-Muller noise
------------------------------------------------------------------------

```c
/* biometric_filter.c
 * CORTEX PROTOCOL — Biometric Normalization Filter (Φ)
 * Target: ARMv8.5-A bare-metal, TrustZone EL1-S
 * Status: SPECIFICATION — Milestone 2 hardware target
 *
 * Implements the Phi operator: Db2 wavelet decomposition +
 * high-frequency coefficient truncation + homeostatic noise injection.
 *
 * Timing guarantee: O(1) constant-time — no data-dependent branches.
 * Spectre/Meltdown mitigations: see barrier placement comments.
 */

#include "keros_types.h"
#include <math.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stddef.h>

/* ── Daubechies-2 analysis filter coefficients ───────────────────────────── */
static const double DB2_H[] = {
     0.34150635052,   /* h0 */
     0.59150635052,   /* h1 */
     0.15849364948,   /* h2 */
    -0.09150635052    /* h3 */
};

#define SIGMA_HOMEOSTATIC 0.045   /* White Branch mandate — do not modify */
#define SIGNAL_LENGTH     512     /* Must match RawBiometricFrame.sample_count max */

/* ── Box-Muller noise generator ──────────────────────────────────────────── *
 * No data-dependent branches. u1, u2 must be pre-sanitized uniform samples
 * from hardware LIMES entropy source (not software PRNG). */
static void generate_homeostatic_noise(
    double *n1, double *n2,
    double u1, double u2)
{
    /* u1 clamped to (0,1] to avoid log(0) — constant-time clamp */
    double u1_safe = u1 + 1e-15;
    double r        = sqrt(-2.0 * log(u1_safe));
    double theta    = 6.28318530717958647692 * u2;   /* 2π — no M_PI dependency */
    *n1 = r * cos(theta) * SIGMA_HOMEOSTATIC;
    *n2 = r * sin(theta) * SIGMA_HOMEOSTATIC;
}

/* ── Main Phi operator ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── *
 * Input:  raw_data      — pointer to frame data in secure SRAM
 *         length        — number of samples (must be even)
 *         entropy_u1/u2 — hardware jitter samples from LIMES
 * Output: purified_data — anonymized signal, safe to export to Phase B
 *
 * INVARIANT: raw_data is zeroed by caller AFTER this function returns.
 * This function does NOT zero raw_data — caller holds that responsibility
 * (context-manager pattern mirrors Python SAL implementation). */
void phi_biometric_filter(
    const double * restrict raw_data,
    double       * restrict purified_data,
    size_t        length,
    double        entropy_u1,
    double        entropy_u2)
{
    if (length == 0 || (length & 1) != 0) return;   /* length must be even */

    double low_coeffs[SIGNAL_LENGTH / 2];
    memset(low_coeffs, 0, sizeof(double) * (length / 2));

    /* ── Phase 1: DWT low-pass pass, high-frequency truncated to zero ── */
    for (size_t i = 0; i < length / 2; i++) {
        double acc = 0.0;
        for (size_t j = 0; j < 4; j++) {
            size_t idx = (i * 2 + j) % length;   /* wrapping — no branch */
            acc += raw_data[idx] * DB2_H[j];
        }
        low_coeffs[i] = acc;
        /* High-frequency coefficients (detail) discarded — never computed.
         * This destroys the individual biometric fingerprint. */
    }

    /* ── Phase 2: Homeostatic noise generation ── */
    double noise_a, noise_b;
    generate_homeostatic_noise(&noise_a, &noise_b, entropy_u1, entropy_u2);

    /* ── Phase 3: Symmetric reconstruction — no individual attractors ── */
    memset(purified_data, 0, sizeof(double) * length);

    for (size_t i = 0; i < length / 2; i++) {
        size_t idx_a = (i * 2)     % length;
        size_t idx_b = (i * 2 + 1) % length;
        purified_data[idx_a] = low_coeffs[i] * DB2_H[0] + noise_a;
        purified_data[idx_b] = low_coeffs[i] * DB2_H[1] + noise_b;
    }

    /* Spectre barrier: prevent speculative reads of low_coeffs after return */
    __asm__ volatile ("dsb sy" ::: "memory");
    __asm__ volatile ("isb"    ::: "memory");
}

```


------------------------------------------------------------------------
G4. matrix_inspector.rs — Shannon entropy validation (LIMES)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

```rust
//! matrix_inspector.rs
//! CORTEX PROTOCOL — LIMES: Silicon Entropy Validation
//! Target: ARMv8.5-A / #[no_std] bare-metal EL1-S
//! Status: SPECIFICATION — Milestone 2 hardware target
//!
//! Validates hardware clock jitter entropy to reject synthetic telemetry.
//! Shannon entropy calculated over nibble histogram of jitter samples.
//!
//! FIX APPLIED (audit 2026-05-18):
//!   - Shannon entropy formula corrected: uses p * ln(p) / ln(2), not p*(p-1)
//!   - libm::log2f used for no_std float log (feature = "libm")
//!   - Constant-time histogram loop: no data-dependent branches

#![no_std]

use core::sync::atomic::{AtomicU32, Ordering};

/* Minimum Shannon entropy in bits for a 256-sample, 16-bucket histogram.
 * At true hardware jitter, expect H ≥ 3.5 bits over nibble distribution.
 * Threshold calibrated by White Branch — do not modify without peer review. */
const MIN_SHANNON_ENTROPY_BITS: f32 = 3.5;

const POOL_SIZE:    usize = 256;
const NUM_BUCKETS:  usize = 16;    /* 4-bit nibble space */

pub struct MatrixInspector {
    entropy_pool: [u32; POOL_SIZE],
    write_ptr:    usize,
}

impl MatrixInspector {
    /// Creates a new inspector with zeroed pool.
    pub const fn new() -> Self {
        Self {
            entropy_pool: [0u32; POOL_SIZE],
            write_ptr:    0,
        }
    }

    /// Ingests a hardware jitter sample (constant-time write, no branch on value).
    pub fn push_jitter_sample(&mut self, sample: u32) {
        let index = self.write_ptr & (POOL_SIZE - 1);   /* bitmask, no branch */
        self.entropy_pool[index] = sample;
        self.write_ptr = self.write_ptr.wrapping_add(1);
    }

    /// Validates pool entropy against MIN_SHANNON_ENTROPY_BITS.
    ///
    /// Returns `true` if entropy is sufficient (biological origin likely).
    /// Returns `false` if entropy is below threshold (synthetic injection suspected).
    ///
    /// Algorithm: Shannon H = -Σ p_i * log2(p_i) over nibble histogram.
    /// Uses libm::log2f for no_std compatibility.
    pub fn verify_silicon_entropy(&self) -> bool {
        let mut counts = [0u32; NUM_BUCKETS];
        let total      = POOL_SIZE as f32;

        /* Build nibble frequency histogram — no data-dependent branches */
        for &sample in self.entropy_pool.iter() {
            let bucket = (sample & 0x0F) as usize;   /* low nibble, 0–15 */
            counts[bucket] = counts[bucket].saturating_add(1);
        }

        /* Shannon entropy: H = -Σ p_i * log2(p_i) */
        let mut entropy: f32 = 0.0;
        for &count in counts.iter() {
            if count > 0 {
                let p = (count as f32) / total;
                /* libm::log2f is available in no_std via the 'libm' crate.
                 * Add to Cargo.toml: libm = { version = "0.2", default-features = false } */
                #[cfg(feature = "libm")]
                {
                    entropy -= p * libm::log2f(p);
                }
                /* Fallback: ln(x)/ln(2) approximation for environments without libm */
                #[cfg(not(feature = "libm"))]
                {
                    /* Taylor: ln(1+x) ≈ x - x²/2 + x³/3 for |x| < 1
                     * This is an approximation — enable libm feature for production */
                    let x    = p - 1.0;
                    let ln_p = x - (x * x) / 2.0 + (x * x * x) / 3.0;
                    let log2_p = ln_p / 0.693_147_2_f32;   /* ln(2) */
                    entropy -= p * log2_p;
                }
            }
        }

        entropy >= MIN_SHANNON_ENTROPY_BITS
    }
}

/* ── Global biological shield state ─────────────────────────────────────── */

pub const STATE_SOMA_SAFE:       u32 = 0x00000001;
pub const STATE_HOMEOSTASIS_LOCK: u32 = 0x00000003;
pub const STATE_DUMMY_CONTAINMENT: u32 = 0x0000007F;

pub static BIOLOGICAL_SHIELD_STATE: AtomicU32 =
    AtomicU32::new(STATE_DUMMY_CONTAINMENT);   /* fail-safe initial state */

/// Evaluates system integrity and updates the biological shield state.
///
/// Called from the FIQ handler after each sensor window.
/// Returns the new shield state value.
#[no_mangle]
pub extern "C" fn evaluate_system_integrity(inspector: &MatrixInspector) -> u32 {
    if !inspector.verify_silicon_entropy() {
        /* Entropy below threshold — possible synthetic signal injection.
         * Transition to HOMEOSTASIS_LOCK and return DUMMY state. */
        BIOLOGICAL_SHIELD_STATE.store(STATE_HOMEOSTASIS_LOCK, Ordering::SeqCst);
        return STATE_DUMMY_CONTAINMENT;
    }

    /* Entropy valid — transition to SAFE if currently in LOCK state */
    let current = BIOLOGICAL_SHIELD_STATE.load(Ordering::SeqCst);
    if current == STATE_HOMEOSTASIS_LOCK {
        /* Do not auto-recover from LOCK — biometric ResProtocol required.
         * This prevents an attacker from momentarily injecting valid entropy
         * to unlock the system. Recovery is handled by resuscitation_kernel. */
        return STATE_DUMMY_CONTAINMENT;
    }

    BIOLOGICAL_SHIELD_STATE.store(STATE_SOMA_SAFE, Ordering::SeqCst);
    STATE_SOMA_SAFE
}

```


------------------------------------------------------------------------
G5. agora_diff_privacy.rs — Laplace LDP (constant-time bitmask)
------------------------------------------------------------------------

```rust
//! agora_diff_privacy.rs
//! CORTEX PROTOCOL — Delta_split: Local Differential Privacy (LDP)
//! Target: ARMv8.5-A / #[no_std] bare-metal
//! Status: SPECIFICATION — Milestone 2 hardware target
//!
//! Implements the Laplace mechanism for the outbound AGORA channel.
//! ε = 0.15, Δf = 1e-3 (White Branch mandate — do not modify).
//!
//! FIX APPLIED (audit 2026-05-18):
//!   - Removed data-dependent if/else in sample_laplace (timing attack).
//!   - Replaced with constant-time bitmask multiplication.
//!   - Input validation added for uniform samples.

#![no_std]

/// Laplace noise parameters — White Branch clinical mandate.
/// ε = 0.15 provides strong privacy for population research donation.
/// b = Δf / ε = 0.001 / 0.15 ≈ 0.006667
pub const EPSILON:      f32 = 0.15;
pub const SENSITIVITY:  f32 = 1e-3;   /* Δf — global sensitivity of the feature */

pub struct AgoraBifurcation {
    epsilon:     f32,
    sensitivity: f32,
}

impl AgoraBifurcation {
    /// Creates a bifurcation operator with the White Branch parameters.
    pub const fn new() -> Self {
        Self {
            epsilon:     EPSILON,
            sensitivity: SENSITIVITY,
        }
    }

    /// Samples Laplace noise for a single uniform input in (0, 1).
    ///
    /// Constant-time version: eliminates the data-dependent if/else
    /// that existed in the previous implementation.
    ///
    /// Laplace inverse CDF: b * sign(u - 0.5) * ln(1 - 2|u - 0.5|)
    /// Rewritten constant-time:
    ///   let v = u - 0.5
    ///   let sign = 1.0 if v >= 0, else -1.0   ← replaced with bitmask
    ///   result = -b * sign * ln(1 - 2*|v|)
    fn sample_laplace_ct(&self, u: f32) -> f32 {
        let scale = self.sensitivity / self.epsilon;   /* b ≈ 0.006667 */
        let v     = u - 0.5_f32;

        /* Constant-time sign: extract sign bit, build ±1.0 without branch.
         * Bit 31 of f32 is the sign bit: 0 → positive, 1 → negative.
         * sign_f32 = +1.0 if v >= 0.0, else -1.0 */
        let v_bits:    u32 = v.to_bits();
        let sign_bit:  u32 = v_bits >> 31;          /* 0 or 1 */
        /* Map 0→+1.0 and 1→-1.0 without branch: 1.0 - 2.0*(sign_bit as f32) */
        let sign_f32:  f32 = 1.0_f32 - 2.0_f32 * (sign_bit as f32);

        let abs_v:     f32 = f32::from_bits(v_bits & 0x7FFF_FFFF);   /* |v| */

        /* Argument to ln: 1 - 2|v|. Clamped to (0,1) to avoid ln(0). */
        let ln_arg: f32 = (1.0_f32 - 2.0_f32 * abs_v).max(1e-7_f32);

        /* ln approximation for no_std — enable libm feature for production */
        #[cfg(feature = "libm")]
        let ln_val: f32 = libm::logf(ln_arg);

        #[cfg(not(feature = "libm"))]
        let ln_val: f32 = {
            /* Taylor: ln(1+x) ≈ x - x²/2 + x³/3 for small x */
            let x = ln_arg - 1.0_f32;
            x - (x * x) / 2.0 + (x * x * x) / 3.0
        };

        -scale * sign_f32 * ln_val
    }

    /// Applies Laplace noise to each element of a feature vector.
    ///
    /// `entropy_source` must contain hardware jitter samples normalized to (0,1).
    /// Provided by LIMES — never use a software PRNG here.
    pub fn apply_delta_split(
        &self,
        features:       &mut [f32],
        entropy_source: &[f32],
    ) {
        if entropy_source.is_empty() {
            return;
        }
        for (i, val) in features.iter_mut().enumerate() {
            let u     = entropy_source[i % entropy_source.len()];
            let noise = self.sample_laplace_ct(u);
            *val += noise;
        }
    }
}

```

G6. blind_switch.s — AArch64 constant-time secure dispatch
------------------------------------------------------------------------

```asm
/* blind_switch.s — AArch64
 * CORTEX PROTOCOL — Constant-time secure dispatch
 * Target: ARMv8.5-A / EL1-S (TrustZone Secure World)
 * Status: SPECIFICATION — Milestone 2 hardware target
 *
 * Performs an indirect branch to a handler without data-dependent
 * conditional jumps. Mitigates Spectre-v2 (branch target injection).
 *
 * Calling convention (AArch64 ABI):
 *   x0 — pointer to manifest/context (passed to handler)
 *   x1 — target handler address (Customs / KEROS gateway)
 *
 * Security properties:
 *   - No conditional branches on biometric data values
 *   - Caller-saved registers zeroed before dispatch
 *   - Full speculation barriers before and after indirect branch
 *   - BTI landing pad at entry (ARM BTI / CFI protection)
 */

.global secure_dispatch_blind
.section .text.secure_dispatch_blind, "ax"
.balign 64       /* Cache-line alignment — prevents false sharing */

secure_dispatch_blind:
    /* BTI 'c' — Branch Target Identification landing pad.
     * Required with -mbranch-protection=bti. Frustrates JOP attacks. */
    hint    #34             /* BTI c (encodable as hint on ARMv8.5) */

    /* 1. Save frame record to secure stack */
    sub     sp,  sp,  #32
    stp     x29, x30, [sp, #16]
    add     x29, sp,  #16

    /* 2. Save manifest pointer; zero volatile registers to prevent
     *    biometric data leakage into the handler's register window */
    mov     x2,  x0          /* save manifest ptr */
    mov     x0,  #0
    mov     x3,  #0
    mov     x4,  #0
    mov     x5,  #0

    /* 3. Full speculation barrier before indirect branch.
     *    DSB SY: complete all memory operations.
     *    ISB:    flush instruction pipeline — forces Spectre-v1 mitigation. */
    dsb     sy
    isb

    /* 4. Restore manifest ptr to x0 for handler (ABI arg0) */
    mov     x0, x2

    /* 5. Indirect branch — constant time, no BTB poisoning path.
     *    x1 holds the pre-validated handler address. */
    br      x1

    /* NOTE: csdb placed HERE is unreachable after 'br x1'.
     * The correct pattern is for each handler to begin with 'csdb'
     * as its first instruction after its own BTI landing pad.
     * See keros_core.c: purge_volatile_registers() for the model. */

    /* Unreachable safe fallthrough */
    ldp     x29, x30, [sp, #16]
    add     sp,  sp,  #32
    ret

```

```markdown
# Layer 1 — Bare-Metal Firmware (Specification)

**Status: SPECIFICATION — Not yet running on real hardware.**  
**Milestone: 2 (Planned)**  
**Target: ARMv8.5-A (Snapdragon 8 Gen 1) / TrustZone EL1-S**

This directory contains the C, Rust, and AArch64 assembly specification for the bare-metal Layer 1 of Cortex Protocol.

## Current Status

| File | Status | Notes |
|------|--------|-------|
| `c/keros_types.h` | Specification | Data structures — aligned, documented |
| `c/biometric_filter.c` | Specification | Phi operator — O(1), no data-dependent branches |
| `c/keros_core.c` | Specification | FIQ handler — constant-time expiry check |
| `rust/matrix_inspector.rs` | Specification | Shannon entropy — corrected formula |
| `rust/agora_diff_privacy.rs` | Specification | Laplace LDP — constant-time (no if/else) |
| `asm/blind_switch.s` | Specification | Secure dispatch — BTI + speculation barriers |
| `linker/keros_secure_enclave.ld` | Specification | TrustZone memory map |

## Known Gaps Before Production

1. **MMIO addresses** in `keros_core.c` are placeholder values. Real addresses require the Snapdragon 8 Gen 1 BSP from Qualcomm.
2. **Falcon-512** signature verification requires an external crate (`pqcrypto-falcon` or equivalent). Not yet integrated.
3. **TPM 2.0 binding** for `keros_seal.py` → bare-metal requires `tpm2-pytss` or `tpm2-tools` integration.
4. **libm feature** in `Cargo.toml` is required for correct Shannon entropy — the fallback Taylor approximation is an approximation only.

## Build (when BSP is available)

```bash
cd src/layer1/rust
rustup target add aarch64-unknown-none
cp .cargo_config_template.toml ../../.cargo/config.toml
cargo build --release --target aarch64-unknown-none
```

See `docs/architecture/ARCHITECTURE.md` for full hardware topology.

```

H1. mvd_range_check.circom — MVD range proof circuit
------------------------------------------------------------------------

```
pragma circom 2.1.6;

// mvd_range_check.circom
// CORTEX PROTOCOL — Layer 2: MVD Zero-Knowledge Range Proof
// Status: FUNCTIONAL — Can be compiled with circom 2.x + snarkjs
//
// Proves: u_min <= v_local <= u_max
// WITHOUT revealing v_local to the verifier (Acolyte).
//
// Uses Poseidon hash for commitment verification (ZK-friendly, no trusted setup).
// Bulletproofs/Ristretto255 is the production target — this Groth16 circuit
// is the current compilable reference implementation.
//
// Compile: circom mvd_range_check.circom --r1cs --wasm --sym
// Prove:   snarkjs groth16 prove mvd_range_check.zkey witness.wtns proof.json public.json

include "./node_modules/circomlib/circuits/comparators.circom";
include "./node_modules/circomlib/circuits/poseidon.circom";

template MVDRangeChecker(n_bits) {
    // ── PUBLIC inputs (known to Acolyte / verifier) ──────────────────────
    signal input u_min;           // Lower homeostatic bound (from White Branch snapshot)
    signal input u_max;           // Upper homeostatic bound
    signal input expected_hash;   // Poseidon commitment: Hash(v_local, blinding_factor)

    // ── PRIVATE inputs (known only to prover / user device) ──────────────
    signal input v_local;         // Purified biometric feature (the secret)
    signal input blinding_factor; // Cryptographic blinding — prevents commitment brute-force

    // ── Internal components ───────────────────────────────────────────────
    component comp_min     = GreaterEqThan(n_bits);
    component comp_max     = LessEqThan(n_bits);
    component hash_verifier = Poseidon(2);

    // ── Constraint 1: Commitment integrity ───────────────────────────────
    // Verifies that v_local matches the committed value.
    // Acolyte can verify commitment without learning v_local.
    hash_verifier.inputs[0] <== v_local;
    hash_verifier.inputs[1] <== blinding_factor;
    hash_verifier.out       === expected_hash;

    // ── Constraint 2: Lower bound (v_local >= u_min) ─────────────────────
    comp_min.in[0] <== v_local;
    comp_min.in[1] <== u_min;
    comp_min.out   === 1;   // R1CS constraint: must be satisfied for valid proof

    // ── Constraint 3: Upper bound (v_local <= u_max) ─────────────────────
    comp_max.in[0] <== v_local;
    comp_max.in[1] <== u_max;
    comp_max.out   === 1;   // If this fails, proof generation fails — no false proofs
}

// Instantiate for 32-bit clinical ranges.
// n_bits = 32 supports normalized clinical values in [0, 4,294,967,295].
// Reduce to n_bits = 16 for wearable devices with constrained prover.
component main {public [u_min, u_max, expected_hash]} = MVDRangeChecker(32);

```

I1. test_cognitive_neutrality.py — Complete test suite
------------------------------------------------------------------------

```python
# ============================================================================
# tests/test_cognitive_neutrality.py
# CORTEX PROTOCOL — Test Suite: Cognitive Neutrality (Steps 1–3)
#
# Run: python3 tests/test_cognitive_neutrality.py
#      (from the cortex-protocol/ root directory)
# ============================================================================

import hashlib, hmac, os, secrets, struct, sys, time

ROOT = os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__)))
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(ROOT, "src", "p2p"))
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(ROOT, "src", "governance"))

from p2p_message_types import (
    CORTEX_MAGIC, CortexMsgType, CortexPacketParser,
    ImmunePatternType, ImmuneSignaturePayload, ImmuneSignatureScope,
    NodeRateLimiter, MAX_PAYLOAD_BYTES,
)
from immune_network import (
    ImmuneNetworkConfig, ImmuneNetworkNode, NodeIdentity,
)
from data_pool import (
    ClinicalDomain, DataPoolWritePort, DataPoolReadPort,
    KAnonymityGate,
)
from white_branch_threshold import (
    GovernanceNodeCredential, GovernanceProposal, NodeJurisdiction,
    ProposalType, WhiteBranchThresholdEngine, sign_proposal,
)

# ── Harness ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
TESTS = []
_passed = _failed = 0
_errors = []

def t(name):
    def decorator(fn):
        TESTS.append((name, fn))
        return fn
    return decorator

def run_all():
    global _passed, _failed
    for name, fn in TESTS:
        try:
            fn()
            _passed += 1
            print(f"  ✅  {name}")
        except AssertionError as e:
            _failed += 1
            _errors.append((name, str(e)))
            print(f"  ❌  {name}  —  {e}")
        except Exception as e:
            _failed += 1
            _errors.append((name, repr(e)))
            print(f"  💥  {name}  —  {type(e).__name__}: {e}")

# ── Shared fixtures ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
SHARED_KEY = secrets.token_bytes(32)
parser     = CortexPacketParser(node_shared_key=SHARED_KEY)
GOV_KEY    = secrets.token_bytes(32)

def _make_node():
    return ImmuneNetworkNode(secrets.token_bytes(32), SHARED_KEY)

def _make_staked_node():
    node = _make_node()
    for _ in range(ImmuneNetworkConfig.MIN_VECTORS_FOR_IMMUNITY):
        node.record_vector_contribution()
    return node

def _make_pool(k=5):
    wp = DataPoolWritePort(governance_key=GOV_KEY, k=k)
    rp = DataPoolReadPort(write_port=wp, governance_key=GOV_KEY)
    return wp, rp

def _proof(bins, cv, bucket):
    return hmac.new(GOV_KEY, bins + struct.pack(">fd", cv, float(bucket)), hashlib.sha256).digest()

def _ingest(wp, domain=ClinicalDomain.CARDIAC_AUTONOMIC, bucket=0, cv=0.25):
    bins = b"\x01" * 32
    return wp.ingest_desci_payload(bins, cv, bucket, domain, _proof(bins, cv, bucket))


# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# STEP 1 — P2P CLOSED VOCABULARY
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

@t("S1-01 Valid ANONYMOUS_VECTOR round-trips through parser")
def _():
    payload = b"\xAB" * 41
    wire    = parser.serialize(CortexMsgType.ANONYMOUS_VECTOR, payload)
    result  = parser.parse(wire)
    assert result is not None
    assert result.msg_type == CortexMsgType.ANONYMOUS_VECTOR
    assert result.payload  == payload

@t("S1-02 Unknown type 0xFF silently dropped — returns None")
def _():
    wire     = parser.serialize(CortexMsgType.ANONYMOUS_VECTOR, b"\x00" * 41)
    bad_wire = bytearray(wire); bad_wire[1] = 0xFF
    assert parser.parse(bytes(bad_wire)) is None

@t("S1-03 Simulated INSTITUTIONAL_ALERT (0xAA) silently dropped")
def _():
    wire     = parser.serialize(CortexMsgType.ANONYMOUS_VECTOR, b"\x00" * 41)
    bad_wire = bytearray(wire); bad_wire[1] = 0xAA
    assert parser.parse(bytes(bad_wire)) is None

@t("S1-04 Wrong magic byte dropped silently")
def _():
    wire     = parser.serialize(CortexMsgType.ANONYMOUS_VECTOR, b"\x00" * 41)
    bad_wire = bytearray(wire); bad_wire[0] = 0x00
    assert parser.parse(bytes(bad_wire)) is None

@t("S1-05 Tampered HMAC (last byte flipped) drops packet")
def _():
    wire     = parser.serialize(CortexMsgType.ANONYMOUS_VECTOR, b"\x00" * 41)
    bad_wire = bytearray(wire); bad_wire[-1] ^= 0xFF
    assert parser.parse(bytes(bad_wire)) is None

@t("S1-06 IMMUNE_SIGNATURE > 256 bytes rejected at serializer")
def _():
    try:
        parser.serialize(CortexMsgType.IMMUNE_SIGNATURE, b"\x00" * 257)
        assert False, "Should raise"
    except ValueError as e:
        assert "256" in str(e)

@t("S1-07 IMMUNE_SIGNATURE exactly 256 bytes accepted")
def _():
    sig = ImmuneSignaturePayload(
        pattern_type=ImmunePatternType.SYNTHETIC_SIGNAL,
        scope=ImmuneSignatureScope.TECHNICAL,
        evidence_hash=secrets.token_bytes(32),
        issuer_nonce=secrets.token_bytes(16),
        first_seen_ts=time.time(), ttl_seconds=3600, sample_count=1,
    )
    wire   = parser.serialize(CortexMsgType.IMMUNE_SIGNATURE, sig.to_bytes())
    result = parser.parse(wire)
    assert result is not None

@t("S1-08 ImmuneSignatureScope COGNITIVE (0x02) does not exist")
def _():
    try:
        ImmuneSignatureScope(0x02); assert False
    except ValueError:
        pass

@t("S1-09 ImmuneSignatureScope POLITICAL (0x04) does not exist")
def _():
    try:
        ImmuneSignatureScope(0x04); assert False
    except ValueError:
        pass

@t("S1-10 ImmuneSignaturePayload TTL > 48h raises ValueError")
def _():
    try:
        ImmuneSignaturePayload(
            pattern_type=ImmunePatternType.REPLAY_ATTACK,
            scope=ImmuneSignatureScope.TECHNICAL,
            evidence_hash=secrets.token_bytes(32),
            issuer_nonce=secrets.token_bytes(16),
            first_seen_ts=time.time(), ttl_seconds=172801, sample_count=1,
        ); assert False
    except ValueError:
        pass

@t("S1-11 Rate limiter allows 3 IMMUNE_SIGNATURE/hour then blocks next 2")
def _():
    lim = NodeRateLimiter(); nid = secrets.token_bytes(32)
    r = [lim.check_and_consume(nid, CortexMsgType.IMMUNE_SIGNATURE) for _ in range(5)]
    assert r[:3] == [True]*3 and r[3:] == [False]*2

@t("S1-12 ANONYMOUS_VECTOR rate limit (3600/h) not exhausted at 100 samples")
def _():
    lim = NodeRateLimiter(); nid = secrets.token_bytes(32)
    for i in range(100):
        assert lim.check_and_consume(nid, CortexMsgType.ANONYMOUS_VECTOR), f"blocked at {i}"

@t("S1-13 Two nodes have independent rate limit counters")
def _():
    lim = NodeRateLimiter()
    na, nb = secrets.token_bytes(32), secrets.token_bytes(32)
    for _ in range(3): lim.check_and_consume(na, CortexMsgType.IMMUNE_SIGNATURE)
    assert lim.check_and_consume(nb, CortexMsgType.IMMUNE_SIGNATURE)

@t("S1-14 Truncated packet returns None")
def _():
    wire = parser.serialize(CortexMsgType.ANONYMOUS_VECTOR, b"\x00" * 41)
    assert parser.parse(wire[:-10]) is None

@t("S1-15 Empty bytes input returns None")
def _():
    assert parser.parse(b"") is None

@t("S1-16 All 6 CortexMsgType values round-trip")
def _():
    for msg_type in CortexMsgType:
        max_sz  = MAX_PAYLOAD_BYTES[msg_type]
        payload = b"\xCC" * min(40, max_sz)
        wire    = parser.serialize(msg_type, payload)
        result  = parser.parse(wire)
        assert result is not None and result.msg_type == msg_type, f"Failed for {msg_type.name}"


# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# STEP 2 — IMMUNE NETWORK ANTI-SYBIL
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

@t("S2-01 Node without stake cannot emit immune signature")
def _():
    assert _make_node().emit_immune_signature(
        ImmunePatternType.SYNTHETIC_SIGNAL, secrets.token_bytes(64)
    ) is None

@t("S2-02 Node with full stake emits immune signature")
def _():
    result = _make_staked_node().emit_immune_signature(
        ImmunePatternType.REPLAY_ATTACK, secrets.token_bytes(64)
    )
    assert result is not None and len(result) > 0

@t("S2-03 Stake activates exactly at MIN_VECTORS_FOR_IMMUNITY boundary")
def _():
    node = _make_node()
    for _ in range(ImmuneNetworkConfig.MIN_VECTORS_FOR_IMMUNITY - 1):
        node.record_vector_contribution()
    assert not node.has_immune_rights
    node.record_vector_contribution()
    assert node.has_immune_rights

@t("S2-04 Unknown type 0xFF dropped by receive_packet")
def _():
    node     = _make_staked_node()
    wire     = parser.serialize(CortexMsgType.ANONYMOUS_VECTOR, b"\x00" * 41)
    bad_wire = bytearray(wire); bad_wire[1] = 0xFF
    assert node.receive_packet(bytes(bad_wire), secrets.token_bytes(32)) is None

@t("S2-05 Signature from unstaked peer not propagated")
def _():
    receiver = _make_staked_node()
    sender   = _make_node()
    receiver.register_peer(NodeIdentity(
        node_id_hash=sender._node_id_hash,
        public_key_bytes=secrets.token_bytes(32),
        contribution_count=0,
        first_seen_ts=time.time(), last_seen_ts=time.time(),
    ))
    emitter  = _make_staked_node()
    sig_wire = emitter.emit_immune_signature(ImmunePatternType.HMAC_FAILURE, secrets.token_bytes(32))
    assert receiver.receive_packet(sig_wire, sender._node_id_hash) is None

@t("S2-06 Threshold K=3: 2 co-signers insufficient — no propagation")
def _():
    a, b, c = _make_staked_node(), _make_staked_node(), _make_staked_node()
    c.register_peer(NodeIdentity(a._node_id_hash, secrets.token_bytes(32), 50, time.time(), time.time()))
    c.register_peer(NodeIdentity(b._node_id_hash, secrets.token_bytes(32), 50, time.time(), time.time()))
    wire = a.emit_immune_signature(ImmunePatternType.SYBIL_PATTERN, secrets.token_bytes(64))
    assert c.receive_packet(wire, a._node_id_hash) is None, "1 cosigner should not propagate"
    assert c.receive_packet(wire, b._node_id_hash) is None, "2 cosigners should not propagate"

@t("S2-07 Staked node rate-limited to 3 immune emissions/hour")
def _():
    node = _make_staked_node()
    r = [node.emit_immune_signature(ImmunePatternType.MALFORMED_PACKET, secrets.token_bytes(32)) for _ in range(5)]
    assert all(x is not None for x in r[:3]) and all(x is None for x in r[3:])

@t("S2-08 Emitted signature stored in local immune memory")
def _():
    node = _make_staked_node()
    ev   = secrets.token_bytes(64)
    node.emit_immune_signature(ImmunePatternType.SYNTHETIC_SIGNAL, ev)
    assert node._immune_mem.knows(hashlib.sha256(ev).digest())

@t("S2-09 Node status dict has all required keys")
def _():
    status = _make_staked_node().get_status()
    for k in ("node_id","has_immune_rights","contribution_count",
              "immune_memory_size","pending_cosignatures","known_peers"):
        assert k in status, f"Missing: {k}"

@t("S3-01 geographic_region query parameter raises ValueError")
def _():
    _, rp = _make_pool()
    try: rp.query("k", geographic_region="EU"); assert False
    except ValueError as e: assert "geographic_region" in str(e)

@t("S3-02 country query parameter raises ValueError")
def _():
    _, rp = _make_pool()
    try: rp.query("k", country="Colombia"); assert False
    except ValueError as e: assert "country" in str(e)

@t("S3-03 lat/lon query parameters raise ValueError")
def _():
    _, rp = _make_pool()
    try: rp.query("k", lat=4.7, lon=-74.0); assert False
    except ValueError as e: assert "lat" in str(e) or "lon" in str(e)

@t("S3-04 age_range demographic parameter raises ValueError")
def _():
    _, rp = _make_pool()
    try: rp.query("k", age_range="20-40"); assert False
    except ValueError as e: assert "age_range" in str(e)

@t("S3-05 4 vectors staged — 0 released before k=5")
def _():
    wp, rp = _make_pool(k=5)
    for _ in range(4): _ingest(wp)
    assert rp.query("k")["count"] == 0

@t("S3-06 5th vector triggers k-anonymity release")
def _():
    wp, rp = _make_pool(k=5)
    for _ in range(5): _ingest(wp)
    assert rp.query("k")["count"] == 5

@t("S3-07 Released vectors carry k_anonymity_group_size == 5")
def _():
    wp, rp = _make_pool(k=5)
    for _ in range(5): _ingest(wp)
    for v in rp.query("k")["vectors"]:
        assert v["k_anonymity_group_size"] == 5

@t("S3-08 Response vectors have no geographic fields")
def _():
    wp, rp = _make_pool(k=5)
    for _ in range(5): _ingest(wp)
    forbidden = {"geographic_region","country","city","lat","lon","region",
                 "demographic","age_range","ethnicity","sex"}
    for v in rp.query("k")["vectors"]:
        assert not (set(v) & forbidden), f"Forbidden fields: {set(v) & forbidden}"

@t("S3-09 Response vectors have no epoch timestamp")
def _():
    wp, rp = _make_pool(k=5)
    for _ in range(5): _ingest(wp)
    for v in rp.query("k")["vectors"]:
        assert "timestamp" not in v
        assert "sequence_counter" in v   # Relative counter is allowed

@t("S3-10 Response vectors have no session_id / user_id / device_id")
def _():
    wp, rp = _make_pool(k=5)
    for _ in range(5): _ingest(wp)
    for v in rp.query("k")["vectors"]:
        for field in ("session_id","user_id","device_id"):
            assert field not in v

@t("S3-11 cognitive_neutrality_notice present in every response")
def _():
    _, rp = _make_pool()
    r = rp.query("k")
    assert "cognitive_neutrality_notice" in r
    assert len(r["cognitive_neutrality_notice"]) > 10

@t("S3-12 Filter by clinical_domain returns only matching domain")
def _():
    wp, rp = _make_pool(k=5)
    for _ in range(5): _ingest(wp, domain=ClinicalDomain.CARDIAC_AUTONOMIC)
    for _ in range(5): _ingest(wp, domain=ClinicalDomain.COGNITIVE_LOAD)
    r = rp.query("k", clinical_domain=ClinicalDomain.CARDIAC_AUTONOMIC)
    assert r["count"] == 5
    for v in r["vectors"]:
        assert v["clinical_domain"] == ClinicalDomain.CARDIAC_AUTONOMIC.value

@t("S3-13 Tampered anonymization proof filtered out when require_proof=True")
def _():
    wp, rp = _make_pool(k=5)
    for _ in range(5): _ingest(wp)
    for entry in wp._public_pool:
        entry.anonymization_proof = secrets.token_bytes(32)
    assert rp.query("k", require_proof=True)["count"] == 0

@t("S3-14 require_proof=False returns vectors regardless of proof validity")
def _():
    wp, rp = _make_pool(k=5)
    for _ in range(5): _ingest(wp)
    assert rp.query("k", require_proof=False)["count"] == 5

@t("S3-15 Ingest with invalid polyvagal_bucket=3 returns False")
def _():
    wp, _ = _make_pool()
    assert wp.ingest_desci_payload(b"\x00"*32, 0.25, 3, ClinicalDomain.CARDIAC_AUTONOMIC, secrets.token_bytes(32)) is False

@t("S3-16 ReadPort serialises to dict — returned JSON has no live object references")
def _():
    # The ReadPort contract: each call to query() returns a new snapshot.
    # The returned dict contains only primitive types (str, float, int) —
    # no live PoolEntry references. Mutating the returned dict cannot affect
    # the pool, and the pool's own mutations are isolated to each query call.
    wp, rp = _make_pool(k=5)
    for _ in range(5): _ingest(wp)
    result = rp.query("k", require_proof=False)
    # The returned vectors are plain dicts — not PoolEntry objects
    for v in result["vectors"]:
        assert isinstance(v, dict), "Vector must be a plain dict, not PoolEntry"
        assert isinstance(v["rmssd_aggregate_cv"], float), "CV must be a primitive float"
    # Mutating the returned dict has no effect on the pool
    original_cv = result["vectors"][0]["rmssd_aggregate_cv"]
    result["vectors"][0]["rmssd_aggregate_cv"] = 999.0
    result2 = rp.query("k", require_proof=False)
    assert result2["vectors"][0]["rmssd_aggregate_cv"] == original_cv,         "Mutating returned dict must not affect subsequent queries"

@t("S3-17 time_window_days=999 is silently clamped — no exception")
def _():
    _, rp = _make_pool()
    r = rp.query("k", time_window_days=999)
    assert "count" in r


# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# BONUS — White Branch Threshold integration
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

def _make_engine_with_one_node():
    engine   = WhiteBranchThresholdEngine()
    priv_key = secrets.token_bytes(32)
    pub_key  = hashlib.sha256(priv_key).digest()
    node_id  = hashlib.sha256(b"test" + pub_key).digest()
    cred     = GovernanceNodeCredential(
        node_id=node_id, public_key=pub_key,
        jurisdiction=NodeJurisdiction.EXAMPLE,
        institution="Test Uni", registered_at=time.time(),
    )
    engine.register_node(cred)
    return engine, node_id, priv_key

@t("WB-01 Clinical threshold proposal without citations rejected")
def _():
    engine, node_id, _ = _make_engine_with_one_node()
    p = GovernanceProposal(
        proposal_id=secrets.token_bytes(16),
        proposal_type=ProposalType.CLINICAL_THRESHOLD_MOD,
        content={"BRIDGE_STD_LIMIT": 0.6}, citations=[],
        proposed_by=node_id, proposed_at=time.time(), expires_at=time.time()+86400,
    )
    ok, msg = engine.submit_proposal(p)
    assert not ok and ("citation" in msg.lower() or "REJECTED" in msg)

@t("WB-02 Valid proposal with peer-reviewed citation accepted (5-node quorum)")
def _():
    # Clinical threshold mod requires N=5 nodes registered — correct behaviour
    engine   = WhiteBranchThresholdEngine()
    proposer_id = None
    jurisdictions = [
        NodeJurisdiction.COLOMBIA, NodeJurisdiction.GERMANY,
        NodeJurisdiction.CANADA,   NodeJurisdiction.INDIA,
        NodeJurisdiction.BRAZIL,
    ]
    for i, jur in enumerate(jurisdictions):
        pk      = secrets.token_bytes(32)
        pub     = hashlib.sha256(pk).digest()
        nid     = hashlib.sha256(f"inst{i}".encode() + pub).digest()
        engine.register_node(GovernanceNodeCredential(
            node_id=nid, public_key=pub, jurisdiction=jur,
            institution=f"Institution {i}", registered_at=time.time(),
        ))
        if i == 0: proposer_id = nid
    p = GovernanceProposal(
        proposal_id=secrets.token_bytes(16),
        proposal_type=ProposalType.CLINICAL_THRESHOLD_MOD,
        content={"BRIDGE_STD_LIMIT": 0.55},
        citations=["Task Force ESC/NASPE (1996). Eur Heart J, 17(3), 354-381."],
        proposed_by=proposer_id, proposed_at=time.time(), expires_at=time.time()+86400,
    )
    ok, msg = engine.submit_proposal(p)
    assert ok, f"Should accept with 5 registered nodes: {msg}"


# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
# MAIN
# ════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

if __name__ == "__main__":
    print("=" * 64)
    print("  Cortex Protocol — Cognitive Neutrality Test Suite")
    print("  Steps 1–3 + White Branch integration")
    print("=" * 64)

    sections = [
        ("STEP 1 — P2P Closed Vocabulary",        [t for t in TESTS if t[0].startswith("S1")]),
        ("STEP 2 — Immune Network Anti-Sybil",     [t for t in TESTS if t[0].startswith("S2")]),
        ("STEP 3 — Data Pool Read-Only Egress",    [t for t in TESTS if t[0].startswith("S3")]),
        ("BONUS  — White Branch Threshold",        [t for t in TESTS if t[0].startswith("WB")]),
    ]

    for title, tests in sections:
        print(f"\n{'─'*64}\n  {title} ({len(tests)} tests)\n{'─'*64}")
        for name, fn in tests:
            try:
                fn()
                _passed += 1
                print(f"  ✅  {name}")
            except AssertionError as e:
                _failed += 1
                _errors.append((name, str(e)))
                print(f"  ❌  {name}  —  {e}")
            except Exception as e:
                _failed += 1
                _errors.append((name, repr(e)))
                print(f"  💥  {name}  —  {type(e).__name__}: {e}")

    total = _passed + _failed
    print(f"\n{'='*64}")
    print(f"  RESULTS: {_passed}/{total} passed", end="")
    if _failed == 0:
        print(" — ALL PASSED ✅")
    else:
        print(f" — {_failed} FAILED ❌")
        for name, err in _errors:
            print(f"\n    ❌ {name}\n       {err}")
    print("=" * 64)
    sys.exit(_failed)

========================================================================
PART J — HARDWARE STATUS & KNOWN LIMITATIONS
========================================================================

J1. WHAT ACTUALLY RUNS TODAY (v0.5.1)
--------------------------------------
ALL execution is Python simulation. No real hardware is connected.

  python3 src/sal/cognitive_shield_v2.py          — full demo (ECDH + CDI + bridge)
  python3 src/sal/cognitive_shield_v2.py --test   — 92 vectors, 0 failures
  python3 -m src.sal.state_buffer_secure           — 9 tests (mlock verified)
  python3 -m src.sal.external_rule_sandbox         — 7 tests (sandbox isolation)
  python3 -m src.keros.sensor_channel              — 7 tests (ECDH crypto verified)
  python3 -m src.keros.bus_to_sal_bridge           — 4 tests (pipeline integration)
  python3 -m src.p2p.p2p_message_types             — 5 tests (closed vocabulary)
  python3 -m src.p2p.data_pool                     — 5 tests (geographic blind spot)
  python3 -m src.p2p.immune_network                — 8 tests (anti-Sybil defense)
  python3 tests/test_cognitive_neutrality.py        — 70 tests (P2P + governance)
  Total tracked: 92 SAL vectors + 70 governance tests = 162 test vectors, 0 failures

WHAT IS SIMULATED:
  - EEG sensor: numpy sine wave + noise (not a real sensor)
  - ECDH bus: Python objects in-process (not a real serial/BLE bus)
  - TEE: Python class (not ARM TrustZone EL1-S)
  - TPM 2.0: not implemented (Milestone 1.5)
  - mlock: REAL (verified working on Linux without root)
  - ctypes zeroing: REAL (secure_zeroize closes OI-007 partially)
  - X25519 ECDH handshake: REAL cryptography (both sides simulated in-process)
  - TelemetryRouter bridge: REAL validation logic (monotone seq, schema, timestamps)

DEVICES THAT COULD WORK WITH A BrainFlow ADAPTER (~100 lines):
  - OpenBCI Cyton (8-ch EEG, 250 Hz, ~$399)
  - Muse 2 (consumer EEG, BLE)
  - Neurosity Crown (wearable EEG)
  These are Milestone 1 targets. No adapter exists yet.

J2. KNOWN LIMITATIONS (from NEUTRALITY.md §4 and SECURITY.md)
--------------------------------------------------------------
[OI-007] CPython heap persistence — PARTIALLY MITIGATED v0.4.5
  mlock prevents swap. ctypes zeroing prevents GC timing gap.
  Kernel copies and cryptography library internals remain uncontrolled.
  Full closure: TPM 2.0 hardware (Milestone 1.5)

[OI-sandbox] Python namespace sandbox, not true WASM
  Current: namespace shadowing via _NoOpProxy/_ForbiddenProxy
  Risk: sophisticated CPython internals abuse
  Full closure: Pyodide or Wasmtime (Milestone 2)

[OI-bus] Physical pin layer not covered by ECDH
  ECDH encrypts the logical bus. ADC output pins before sensor firmware
  are still readable with physical access.
  Full closure: Sensor MCU with TrustZone-M (Milestone 1.5)

[OI-whitebranch] White Branch is a human institution
  Can be captured over multi-decade horizon.
  Mitigated by: ≥3 jurisdictions quorum, public audit trail, 48h propagation delay.
  Not fully closeable by architecture — acknowledged openly.

[OI-limes] LIMES entropy distinguishability
  Assumes biological entropy is statistically distinguishable from synthetic.
  Valid today. Subject to annual review as generative AI advances.

J3. OPEN ITEMS — v0.5.2 BACKLOG
---------------------------------
The following items were not blocking for v0.5.1 and are carried forward:

[J3.4] requirements.txt: add scipy>=1.11,<2.0 version pin
       Risk: future scipy releases may change hilbert() behavior.
       Estimate: ~15 minutes.

[OI-ECDH-persistence] Session key is Python bytes object
       After full_handshake(), the derived session_key is a Python bytes
       object on the CPython heap. mlock does not cover it without wrapping
       in SecureKeyBuffer. To fully close: wrap session_key in SecureKeyBuffer
       and pass as export_bytearray() to callers. Estimate: ~1h.

[OI-p2p-transport] p2p_transport.py real UDP layer
       P2P messaging currently uses in-memory queues. Real UDP transport
       with DTLS/QUIC encryption is Milestone 1 scope.

BLOCKING ITEMS FOR v1.0 (production):
1. Clinical validation study (≥20 participants, real EEG/HRV)
2. First independent Governance Node (GPG key registered)
3. Layer 1 on real ARMv8.5 hardware with TPM 2.0
4. WASM sandbox replacing Python namespace isolation
5. IEEE P2510 or equivalent standards engagement
6. BrainFlow adapter (~100 lines, connects OpenBCI/Muse 2 to SAL)

================================================================================
  END OF CORTEX PROTOCOL v0.5.1 COMPLETE REFERENCE
================================================================================
